 report ke anusaar mote logon jinka biemai (25-30 kilogram prati varg meter) tha unamem saamaanya biemai (20-25 kilogram prati varg meter) vaale logon kii tulana main dil kii bimariyon kii vajah se maut kaa khatra sabase kam paaya gaya

 )(hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) nepalmein shanivaar ko aae bheeshan bukamp main gorkha jile kaa saurapani gaanv bhi puri tarah tabah ho chukaa tha
 Sun Kumari Gurung, who lives in the same village, was also demolished due to the earthquake
 9 maheene kaa garbh liye sunkumari apane hi ghar ke toote malbe main behosh padi thi
 At six o'clock in the evening, the local villagers took Sun Kumari out of the rubble and took it to the nearby Torong forest due to the frequent earthquakes, where Sun Kumari gave birth to a daughter in a cave in Torong forest, but at that time Neither he had any medicines nor nurses
 sun kumari ne bataaya kibacchike janm ke samay na to uske paas khaane kii koi cheez thi, naa senkane ke liye garm pani dawaai to bahut dur kii baat he
 Sunkumari told four days just by drinking water
 buudhvaar ko jab uske gaanv main helicapter pahunchaa to us mahila ko gorkha jila aspataal main bhartee karaayaa gaya
 Sun Kumari is fine, but her newborn daughter has jaundice and is undergoing treatment
 vahaan doctoron ne bacchee kaa upachaar nahin ho paane kii baat kah di he
 Sunakumari said that he has neither money nor any means, so that he can go to another hospital for treatment
 malbe main dabe hone ke kaaran khud sunkumari kaa donon paanv buree tarah jakhmi he
 She herself cannot even walk and her newborn baby is becoming more ill due to lack of treatment
 sunkumari ne apni beti kaa naam bhuinchampa rakhaa he
 Earthquake in Nepali is called Bhuinchalo
 chunki bhucamp ke din usne beti ko janm diya isliye apni beti ko vah bhuinchampa kahkar pukaarti he
 Recognizing that the opportunities for government jobs are shrinking and the private sector is expanding, the central government said on Saturday that it is constantly negotiating for reservation in jobs in the private sector
 saamaajik nyaay or aadhikarita mantri kumari sailaja ne loksabhaa main ‘samvidhan (anusuchit jatiyaan) aadesh (sanshodhan) vidheyak 2012’ par hui charchaa kaa jawaab dete hue yah baat kahi
 The House passed this bill by voice
 unhone vidheyak par charchaa main bhaag lene vaale sadasyon kii is chintaa se sahmati jataai ki nijee kshetra main naukariyon main anusuchit jatiyon ke liye aarakshan kaa praavdhaan nahin hone se gambhir samasyaayein paidaa ho sakati hai
 Salja said that letters have been written to the private sector several times in this regard and the government wants the private sector to somehow realize how serious this issue is
 unhone kaha ki nijee kshetra ne is mudde ko gambhirtha se nahin liya to iske kaaphi dushprinaam ho sakate hai
 When demanded by the bsp's Dara Singh Chauhan to take tough steps in this regard, Salja said that the government wants that strict steps should not be taken and it would be better for the private sector to accept this thing comfortably
 isse pehle charchaa kii shuruyaat karte hue bhaajapa ke virendra kashyap ne kaha ki koun anusuchit jati kaa he or koun nahin, is mudde ke samaadhaan ke liye ek niti banani chahie
 He also appealed for the provision of reservation for people of this caste in the judiciary
 congress ke piel punia ne kaha ki nijee kshetra main naukariyon ke adhik avasar hai or isiilie anusuchit jatiyon ko is kshetra main aarakshan milanaa chahie
 The bill was introduced by Social Justice Minister Kumari Selja on 5 August
 sapa ke shailendra kumaar ne kaha ki essi yaa asti ko suvidhaayen nahin milane ke kaaran hi ve log essi se asti yaa asti se essi main jane kii maang karte hai
 bsp's Baliram stated the need to amend the constitution for reservation in the private sector
 janata dal you ke bhoodev choudhary ne kaha ki essi or asti ke 80 fisadi bachche abhi bhi kuposhan kaa shikaar hai jisaki vajah se ve viklaangata or beemaari se grasit rahete hai
 The comments trinmul congress ke saugat raay or makapa ke mohan malik ne bhi nijee kshetra main aarakshan kii jarurat bataai
 Mohan Jena of BJD said that traditional industries are disappearing and due to this people of Anu caste and tribe are facing more problems
 bhakpa ke prabodh pandas, neshnal conference ke esady shariq, aal india majalis e ittehadul musalamin ke asaduddin owesi, jharkhand vikaas morcha (prajatantric) ke ajay kumaar, rajd ke raghuvansh prasad singh, ralod ke sanjay singh chouhan, bhaajapa ke virendra kumaar tathaa congress ke aar dhruvanarayan ne bhi charchaa main hissaa liya
 Social Justice and Empowerment Minister Kumari Selja said this while replying to the discussion on 'constitution (scheduled Castes) Order (amendment) Bill 2012' in Lok Sabha
 sadan ne is vidheyak ko dhvanimat se paarit kar diya
 He agreed with the concern of the members participating in the discussion on the Bill that non-provision of reservation for Scheduled Castes in jobs in the private sector can cause serious problems
 sailaja ne bataaya ki nijee sector ko is sambandh main kai baar chitthiyaan likhi gai hai or sarkaar chaahati he ki nijee kshetra kisi na kisi tarah se khud is baat ko mahasoos kare ki yah kitna gambhir mudda he
 He said that if the private sector did not take this issue seriously then it could have many consequences
 basapa ke darasingh chouhan dwaara is sambandh main kade kadam uthaae jane kii maang kiye jane par sailaja ne kaha ki sarkaar chaahati he ki kade kadam nahin uthaane paden or acha hoga ki nijee kshetra aaraam se is baat ko maan jaae
 Earlier, starting the discussion, bjp's Virendra Kashyap said that a policy should be formulated to address the issue of who belongs to the Scheduled Castes and who does not
 unhone nyaaypalika main bhi is jati ke logon ke liye aarakshan kaa praavdhaan kiye jane kii apil kii
 PL Poonia of the Congress said that there are more job opportunities in the private sector and that is why the Scheduled Castes should get reservation in this area
 is vidheyak ko saamaajik nyaay mantri kumari sailaja ne 5 agast ko pesh kiya tha
 sp's Shailendra Kumar said that due to lack of facilities to SC or ST, they demand to go from SC to ST or ST to SC
 basapa ke baliram ne nijee kshetra main aarakshan ke liye samvidhan main sanshodhan kii jarurat bataai
 Bhudev Chaudhary of the Janata Dal UK said that 80 percent of SC and ST children are still malnourished due to which they suffer from disability and disease
 tippaniyan Saugata Roy of Trinamool Congress and Mohan Malik of CPI (M) also expressed the need for reservation in the private sector
 bijd ke mohan jena ne kaha ki paramparaagat udyog lupt ho rahe hai or iske chalate anu jati or janajati ke logon ko adhik pareshaaniyon kaa saamana karnaa pad rahaa he
 Prabodh Panda of CPI, SD Sharik of National Conference, Asaduddin Owaisi of All India Majlis a Ittehadul Muslimeen, Ajay Kumar of Jharkhand Vikas Morcha (prajatantrik), Raghuvansh Prasad Singh of RJD, Sanjay Singh Chauhan of RLD, Virendra Kumar of BJP and Congress R
 Dhruvanarayan also participated in the discussion

 diwali (diwali 2018) hinduon kaa sabase bada tyohaar he

e

 diwali par pujan ke liye saamagrimahalakshmi pujan main kesar, roli, chaaval, paan kaa patta, supaari,fal, phool, doodh, khil, bataashe, sindur, sookhe mewa, mithai, dahi gangaajal dhoop, agarbatti , deepak rui, kalava, nariyal or kalash ke liye ek tambe kaa paatr
 Know what things to worship 
 
 1
 On the day of worship, first of all, put red or yellow cloth on a big and clean outpost and keep the idols of lakshmi-ganesh installed on it
 dhyaan rahe ki unka mukh purv yaa pashchim main rahe

 2
 All the people who worship worship sit in front of the idols
 3
 Now place a kalash on the rice near Lakshmi
 kalash ke upar ek nariyal ko laal vastra main is prakaar lapet kar rakhen ki nariyal kaa agrabhag dikhaai detaa rahe
 3
 yah kalash varun kaa pratik hota he
 Near the Kalash, see two large lamp, one with ghee and the other with oil lamp
 ek deepak chaowkee ke dayee ore rakhen or doosraa murtiyon ke charnon main
 Keep a lamp near Ganesh ji
 4
 Put a small cloth on the front of the garrison and put red cloth on it
 kalash kii ore ek mutthi chaaval se laal vastra par navagraha ke pratik banaaen
 5
 ganeshji kii ore chaaval kii solah pratik banaaen jinhen maatrakaa kaa pratik mana jaataa hai

 6
 Now place betel nut in the middle of it

 thaaliyon main puja kii in jaruri chizon ko rakhen- gyaarah deepak
